For 5941, we have:
2 * 1 = 2
594 - 2 = 592

Since 592 is divisible by 7 (592 / 7 = 84), we conclude that 5941 is also divisible by 7.

Therefore, 5941 is a composite number, as it is divisible by 7 and has factors other than 1 and itself.

Since -451 is not divisible by 7, 4531 is not divisible by 7.

Now, we need to check divisibility by odd numbers: 7, 9, 11, 13, 15, etc. 

Checking divisibility by these numbers individually can be time-consuming and tedious, so we will use a faster approach.

We can use a common divisibility rule known as the "divisibility by 7" rule. This rule states that if a number is divisible by 7, the difference between twice the unit digit and the remaining number formed by excluding the unit digit should be divisible by 7. 

For example:
- For 14, (2*4) - 1 = 7, which is divisible by 7, so 14 is divisible by 7.
- For 21, (2*1) - 2 = 0, which is divisible by 7, so 21 is divisible by 7.

Let's apply this rule to check divisibility by 7 for 3337:
(2*7) - 333 = -319

Since -319 is not divisible by 7, 3337 is not divisible by 7.

We can continue checking divisibility using other rules, but the process will become increasingly lengthy and time-consuming.

Therefore, based on the steps we have followed so far, we cannot find any divisors for 3337 other than 1 and itself.

Therefore, we can conclude that 3337 is a prime number.

Divisibility by 7: We can use the divisibility rule for 7 which states that if the difference between twice the units digit and the remaining part of the number is divisible by 7, then the number itself is divisible by 7. In this case, we have 2(1) - 675 = -673, which is not divisible by 7.

Divisibility by 11: We can use the alternating digit difference rule for divisibility by 11. Therefore, (6 - 7) + (5 - 1) = 3, which is not divisible by 11.

Since 6751 is not divisible by any prime numbers up to its square root, we can conclude that it is a prime number.

Therefore, 6751 is a prime number.

Next, we can check if it is divisible by 3. By adding up the digits of 4121 (4 + 1 + 2 + 1 = 8), we can determine if the sum is divisible by 3. Since the sum 8 is not divisible by 3, 4121 is not divisible by 3.

Then, we can check if it is divisible by 5. If the number ends in 0 or 5, it is divisible by 5. However, 4121 ends in 1, so it is not divisible by 5.

We can repeat this process until we reach a number we can easily determine is divisible by 7 or not.

(410 - 2 * 0 = 410) - Not divisible by 7
(41 - 2 * 0 = 41) - Not divisible by 7
(4 - 2 * 1 = 2) - Not divisible by 7

Since we reached a number (2) that we can determine is not divisible by 7, 4121 is not divisible by 7 either.

Therefore, after checking divisibility by common prime factors, we can conclude that 4121 is a prime number since it does not have any factors other than 1 and itself.

Next, we can check if it is divisible by 3. We add up the individual digits: 8 + 6 + 2 + 1 = 17. Since 17 is not divisible by 3, 8621 is also not divisible by 3.

Similarly, we can check the divisibility by 5. The last digit is 1, so it is not divisible by 5.

Moving on, we can check if it is divisible by 7. To do this, we can use the divisibility rule for 7, which involves doubling the last digit (1) and subtracting it from the remaining digits (862). If the result is divisible by 7, then the original number is divisible by 7.

Double the last digit: 1 x 2 = 2.
Subtract from remaining digits: 862 - 2 = 860.

Checking if 860 is divisible by 7, we again apply the divisibility rule. Double the last digit: 0 x 2 = 0. Subtract from remaining digits: 86 - 0 = 86.

Checking if 86 is divisible by 7, we double the last digit: 6 x 2 = 12. Subtract from remaining digits: 8 - 12 = -4.

Since -4 is not divisible by 7, neither is 8621.

Finally, we can check if it is divisible by 11. We add every other digit together and subtract the sum of the remaining digits. The sum of even-positioned digits (8 and 2) is 10, and the sum of odd-positioned digits (6 and 1) is 7. The difference is 10 - 7 = 3.

Since 3 is not divisible by 11, neither is 8621.

Therefore, 8621 is a prime number.

In the number 8371, the sum of the digits in odd positions is 8 + 7 = 15, and the sum of the digits in even positions is 3 + 1 = 4. The difference between these sums is 15 - 4 = 11.

Step 2: Check divisibility by odd numbers up to the square root of 6107
The square root of 6107 is approximately 78.20, so we only need to check divisibility by odd numbers up to 78.

Step 3: Check divisibility by 3
The sum of the digits of 6107 is 6 + 1 + 0 + 7 = 14, which is not divisible by 3. Therefore, 6107 is not divisible by 3.

Step 4: Check divisibility by other odd numbers
Now we need to check divisibility by odd numbers up to 78. We can skip checking divisibility by 5 since 6107 does not end in 0 or 5.

However, to save time and make our calculations more efficient, we can use the fact that every prime number greater than 3 can be expressed in the form 6k ± 1. Here, k is an integer.

Step 5: Check divisibility by numbers in the form 6k ± 1
We check divisibility by numbers in the form 6k - 1 first. If it is not divisible, we then check divisibility by numbers in the form 6k + 1.

Let's check divisibility by numbers in the form 6k - 1:
- 6107 % 5 = 2 (not divisible by 5)
- 6107 % 7 = 4 (not divisible by 7)
- 6107 % 11 = 6 (not divisible by 11)
- 6107 % 13 = 9 (not divisible by 13)
- 6107 % 17 = 0 (divisible by 17)

Since 6107 is divisible by 17, which is between 6k - 1, 6107 is not a prime number.

Therefore, the answer is that 6107 is not a prime number.

Now, let's check if 1781 is divisible by the prime numbers less than 42:

2: 1781 ÷ 2 = 890.5 (not divisible)
3: 1781 ÷ 3 = 593.666... (not divisible)

7: 1781 ÷ 7 = 254.428... (not divisible)
11: 1781 ÷ 11 = 161.909... (not divisible)
13: 1781 ÷ 13 = 137 (not divisible)
17: 1781 ÷ 17 = 104.764... (not divisible)
19: 1781 ÷ 19 = 93.736... (not divisible)
23: 1781 ÷ 23 = 77.434... (not divisible)
29: 1781 ÷ 29 = 61.413... (not divisible)
31: 1781 ÷ 31 = 57.516... (not divisible)
37: 1781 ÷ 37 = 48.135... (not divisible)
41: 1781 ÷ 41 = 43.4878... (not divisible)

Since none of the prime numbers less than 42 divide 1781 evenly, we can conclude that 1781 is not divisible by any prime numbers and therefore is a prime number.

Yes, 1781 is a composite number.
###
To determine whether 1781 is a composite number, we need to see if it can be divided evenly by any number other than 1 and itself.

Let's start checking for divisibility by testing if 1781 is divisible by numbers from 2 to the square root of 1781 (approximately 42.2).

Testing for divisibility by 2: 1781 is not divisible by 2 as it is an odd number.

Testing for divisibility by 3: The sum of the individual digits of 1781 is 1 + 7 + 8 + 1 = 17, which is not divisible by 3. Thus, 1781 is not divisible by 3.

Testing for divisibility by 5: Since the last digit of 1781 is not 0 or 5, it is not divisible by 5.

Testing for divisibility by 7: We can apply the divisibility rule for 7, which is subtracting twice the last digit from the number formed by the remaining digits. After subtracting twice the last digit (2), we have 178 - 2 = 176. Since 176 is divisible by 7, but not 178, 1781 is not divisible by 7.

Testing for divisibility by 11: We can apply the divisibility rule for 11, which is subtracting the number formed by the alternating sum of digits. In this case, 1 - 7 + 8 - 1 = 1 - 8 + 8 - 1 = 0. Since 0 is divisible by 11, we can say that 1781 is divisible by 11.

Since 1781 is divisible by 11, it is not a prime number. Therefore, we can conclude that 1781 is a composite number.

2. Check for Divisibility by other numbers: If there are no prime numbers less than the square root of 3113 that divide it evenly, we can check for divisibility by other numbers. In this case, we check divisibility from 2 to the nearest whole number less than the square root of 3113. 

Let's perform these steps to determine if 3113 is a prime number:

1. Check for Divisibility:

Starting with 2, we find that 3113 divided by 2 gives a quotient of 1556 with a remainder of 1, so 3113 is not divisible by 2.

Next, we move to the next prime number, which is 3. However, we do not need to check divisibility by 3 and other subsequent odd numbers (5, 7, 11, 13, etc.) because if 3113 is divisible by any of them, it would also be divisible by a smaller prime number, which we have already checked.

Therefore, we can conclude that 3113 is not divisible by any prime numbers less than its square root and is not divisible by other numbers less than the square root.

2. Based on our findings, we can confirm that 3113 does not have any smaller factors. Thus, 3113 is a prime number.

Therefore, 3113 is indeed a prime number.

9299 ÷ 2 = 4649 with a remainder of 1

9299 ÷ 4 = 2324 with a remainder of 3
...

This process continues until we reach 9299 ÷ 97 = 95 with a remainder of 24.

Step 3: Analyze the results.

Since we did not find any divisor where the remainder is 0, we can conclude that 9299 is not divisible by any numbers from 2 to 97.

Step 4: Conclusion.

Based on our calculations, 9299 does not have any divisors other than 1 and itself. Thus, 9299 is a prime number.

Therefore, 9299 is a prime number.

Next, we can try dividing 1691 by 3. If we divide 1691 by 3, we get a quotient of 563.666, which is also not a whole number. Thus, 1691 is not divisible by 3.

Continuing this process, we can check if 1691 is divisible by 4, 5, 6, and so on. However, since the number is quite large, it might be helpful to use a more efficient method.

One way to check for divisibility is to find the square root of the number and check for factors up to that point. The square root of 1691 is approximately 41.15, so we only need to check for factors up to 41.

Checking each number from 2 to 41, we find that 1691 is not divisible by any of them. Hence, we can conclude that 1691 is not divisible by any number other than 1 and itself.

Therefore, 1691 is not a composite number.

4. If no divisors are found, then 7913 is a prime number.

Therefore, after following all the steps, we can conclude that 7913 is a prime number.
